        function Nevermiss:CSync()
            Important["CFrameVisualize"].Parent = Config['Anti Aim'].CFrame.Visuals.Enabled and Config['Anti Aim'].CFrame.Visuals.Clone and Config['Anti Aim'].CFrame.Enabled and Important.IgnoreFolder or nil
            if ( Config['Anti Aim'].CFrame.Enabled and LocalPlayer['Character'] and LocalPlayer['Character']['HumanoidRootPart'] ) then
            local FakeCFrame = LocalPlayer['Character']['HumanoidRootPart'].CFrame;
            Saved = LocalPlayer['Character']['HumanoidRootPart'].CFrame;
            local attach = (Config['Anti Aim'].CFrame.Config.Attach and Target and Target['Character'] and Target['Character']['HumanoidRootPart']) or LocalPlayer['Character']['HumanoidRootPart']
            local attach2 = LocalPlayer['Character']['HumanoidRootPart']
            if ( Config['Anti Aim'].CFrame['Randomized'].Enabled and Flags.randomenabled ) then
                FakeCFrame = attach.CFrame + Vector3.new(math.random(-Config['Anti Aim'].CFrame['Randomized'].Value[1], Config['Anti Aim'].CFrame['Randomized'].Value[1]), math.random(-0, Config['Anti Aim'].CFrame['Randomized'].Value[2]), math.random(-Config['Anti Aim'].CFrame['Randomized'].Value[3], Config['Anti Aim'].CFrame['Randomized'].Value[3]))
            end
            if ( Config['Anti Aim'].CFrame['Player Offset'].Enabled and Flags.offsetenabled ) then
                FakeCFrame = attach.CFrame * CFrame.new(Config['Anti Aim'].CFrame['Player Offset'].Value[1], Config['Anti Aim'].CFrame['Player Offset'].Value[2], Config['Anti Aim'].CFrame['Player Offset'].Value[3])
            end
            if ( Config['Anti Aim'].CFrame['Destroy Cheaters'].Enabled and Flags.destroyenabled ) then
                FakeCFrame = attach2.CFrame * CFrame.new(9e9, 0/0, math.huge)
            end
            if ( Config['Anti Aim'].CFrame['Void Spam'].Enabled and Flags.voidenabled ) then
                 FakeCFrame = voidspamshi and attach2.CFrame * CFrame.new(9e9, 0/1, math.huge) or attach2.CFrame
            end
            
            Important['CFrameVisualize']:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(FakeCFrame)

            LocalPlayer['Character']['HumanoidRootPart'].CFrame = FakeCFrame
            --
            Services.RunService.RenderStepped:Wait()
            --
            CameraPart.Position = Saved.Position+Vector3.new(0,1.5,0)
            Camera.CameraSubject = CameraPart
            LocalPlayer['Character']['HumanoidRootPart'].CFrame = Saved
            end
        end

        function Nevermiss:TargetPosition() 
        if Target then
            local HumanoidRootPart = Target['Character']['HumanoidRootPart']
            local Hit = HumanoidRootPart.CFrame

            local PlayerVelocity = Config.Combat.Resolver.Enabled and (Important.Resolver.ResolvedVelocity + Target['Character']['Humanoid'].MoveDirection * Target['Character']['Humanoid'].MoveDirection) or HumanoidRootPart.Velocity

            local PredictionOffset = Vector3.new(PlayerVelocity.X * Config.Combat.Prediction.Value[1], math.clamp(PlayerVelocity.Y * Config.Combat.Prediction.Value[2], -10, 9999), PlayerVelocity.Z * Config.Combat.Prediction.Value[3])

            local PredictedPosition = Hit + (PredictionOffset * Vector3.new(Config.Combat.Prediction.Multiplier[1], Config.Combat.Prediction.Multiplier[2], Config.Combat.Prediction.Multiplier[3]))

            return PredictedPosition
        end
        end

function Nevermiss:Resolve()
    if Config.Combat.Enabled and Config.Combat.Resolver.Enabled and Target and Target.Character then

        local function Lerp(A, B, T)
            return A * (1 - T) + B * T
        end

        -- Get HumanoidRootPart
        local HumanoidRootPart = Target.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        if not HumanoidRootPart then return end

        -- Initialize storage
        Important.Resolver.PositionHistory = Important.Resolver.PositionHistory or {}
        Important.Resolver.TimeHistory = Important.Resolver.TimeHistory or {}
        Important.Resolver.ResolvedVelocity = Important.Resolver.ResolvedVelocity or Vector3.zero
        Important.Resolver.Kalman = Important.Resolver.Kalman or {P = 1, Q = 0.02, R = 0.1}

        -- Get current time and position
        local CurrentTime = os.clock()
        local CurrentPosition = HumanoidRootPart.Position

        -- Store position and time history
        table.insert(Important.Resolver.PositionHistory, CurrentPosition)
        table.insert(Important.Resolver.TimeHistory, CurrentTime)

        -- Keep history manageable (limit to 50 entries)
        if #Important.Resolver.PositionHistory > 50 then
            table.remove(Important.Resolver.PositionHistory, 1)
            table.remove(Important.Resolver.TimeHistory, 1)
        end

        -- Get previous position and time
        local PreviousPosition = Important.Resolver.PositionHistory[#Important.Resolver.PositionHistory - 1] or CurrentPosition
        local PreviousTime = Important.Resolver.TimeHistory[#Important.Resolver.TimeHistory - 1] or CurrentTime

        -- Calculate delta time
        local DeltaTime = math.max(CurrentTime - PreviousTime, 1e-6)

        -- Calculate raw velocity
        local RawVelocity = (CurrentPosition - PreviousPosition) / DeltaTime

        -- **Replication System: Detect Large CFrame Modifications**
        local PositionDelta = (CurrentPosition - PreviousPosition).Magnitude
        if PositionDelta > Config.Combat.Resolver.JitterThreshold then -- Adjust threshold based on expected movement range
            CurrentPosition = PreviousPosition + RawVelocity * DeltaTime -- Predict a more natural position
        end

        -- Choose smoothing method
        local SmoothingMethod = Config.Combat.Resolver.SmoothingMethod or "Lerp"
        local Smoothness = math.clamp(Config.Combat.Resolver.Smoothness or 0.5, 0.01, 1)

        local function ApplySmoothing(Previous, Raw, T)
            local SmoothedValue

            if SmoothingMethod == "Lerp" then
                SmoothedValue = Lerp(Previous, Raw, T)

            elseif SmoothingMethod == "Exponential" then
                SmoothedValue = Previous + (Raw - Previous) * (1 - math.exp(-T * 5))

            elseif SmoothingMethod == "MovingAverage" then
                local Sum = Vector3.zero
                local Count = math.min(#Important.Resolver.PositionHistory, 10)
                for I = 1, Count do
                    Sum = Sum + (Important.Resolver.PositionHistory[#Important.Resolver.PositionHistory - I] or Vector3.zero)
                end
                SmoothedValue = Sum / Count

            elseif SmoothingMethod == "MedianFilter" then
                local Sorted = {}
                for I = math.max(1, #Important.Resolver.PositionHistory - 5), #Important.Resolver.PositionHistory do
                    table.insert(Sorted, Important.Resolver.PositionHistory[I])
                end
                table.sort(Sorted, function(A, B) return A.Magnitude < B.Magnitude end)
                SmoothedValue = Sorted[math.ceil(#Sorted / 2)] or Raw

            elseif SmoothingMethod == "KalmanFilter" then
                local K = Important.Resolver.Kalman.P / (Important.Resolver.Kalman.P + Important.Resolver.Kalman.R)
                SmoothedValue = Previous + K * (Raw - Previous)
                Important.Resolver.Kalman.P = (1 - K) * Important.Resolver.Kalman.P + Important.Resolver.Kalman.Q

            elseif SmoothingMethod == "WeightedAverage" then
                SmoothedValue = (Previous * 0.7 + Raw * 0.3)

            elseif SmoothingMethod == "Adaptive" then
                local AdaptiveT = math.clamp((Raw - Previous).Magnitude * 0.05, 0.05, 0.5)
                SmoothedValue = Lerp(Previous, Raw, AdaptiveT)

            elseif SmoothingMethod == "Momentum" then
                SmoothedValue = Previous * 0.85 + Raw * 0.15

            elseif SmoothingMethod == "Cosine" then
                SmoothedValue = Previous + (Raw - Previous) * (0.5 - 0.5 * math.cos(T * math.pi))

            elseif SmoothingMethod == "ExponentialDecay" then
                SmoothedValue = Previous * math.exp(-T * 0.5) + Raw * (1 - math.exp(-T * 0.5))

            else
                SmoothedValue = Raw
            end

            return SmoothedValue
        end

        -- Apply smoothing method
        Important.Resolver.ResolvedVelocity = ApplySmoothing(Important.Resolver.ResolvedVelocity, RawVelocity, Smoothness)

        -- Ensure velocity isn't stuck at zero
        if Important.Resolver.ResolvedVelocity.Magnitude < 1e-4 then
            Important.Resolver.ResolvedVelocity = RawVelocity
        end

        -- Update stored values
        Important.Resolver.OldPos = CurrentPosition
        Important.Resolver.OldTick = CurrentTime
    end
end

        function Nevermiss:LookAt()
            if Config.Combat.Enabled and Config.Combat.LookAt and Target and LocalPlayer and LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid then
                LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.AutoRotate = false
                LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Position, Vector3.new(Target.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.X, LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Position.Y, Target.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Z))
            else
                LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.AutoRotate = true
            end
        end


        function Nevermiss:Hitcham(Player, Color)
            local Character = Player['Character']
            local RootPart  = Character and Character:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart')
                    Character.Archivable  = true
                    local Clone = Character:Clone()
                    Clone.Parent = Visuals.EtherealParts
                    Clone.Humanoid.DisplayDistanceType = Enum.HumanoidDisplayDistanceType.None
                    local Highlight = Instance.new('Highlight')
                    Highlight.Parent = Clone
                    Highlight.FillColor = Color
                    Highlight.OutlineColor = Color
                    Highlight.OutlineTransparency = 0
                    Highlight.FillTransparency = 0.5
                    Highlight.DepthMode = Enum.HighlightDepthMode.Occluded
                    Highlight.Adornee = Clone
                    for _, v in pairs(Clone:GetDescendants()) do
                        if ( (v:IsA('MeshPart')) ) then
                            v.Material = Enum.Material.ForceField
                            v.Color = Color
                            v.CanCollide = false
                            v.Anchored = true
                            v.CanQuery = false
                            v.CanTouch = false
                        end
  
                        if ( (v:IsA('Accessory') or v:IsA('Tool')) ) then
                            v:Destroy()
                        end
                    end
  
                    for i,v in pairs(Character:GetDescendants()) do
                        if ( (v:IsA('MeshPart')) ) then
                            local ClonePart = Clone:FindFirstChild(v.Name)
  
                            if ( (ClonePart) ) then
                                ClonePart.CFrame = v.CFrame
                            end
                        end
                    end
  
            Clone:PivotTo(Character.PrimaryPart.CFrame + Vector3.new(LocalPlayer['Character']['HumanoidRootPart'].CFrame.lookVector.x * 1.5, 0, LocalPlayer['Character']['HumanoidRootPart'].CFrame.lookVector.z * 1.5))
  
            Character.Archivable = false
            local tween
            local total_time = 0

            tween = Nevermiss:Connection(Services.RunService.Heartbeat, function(delta_time)
                total_time += delta_time
                local fadeValue = Services.TweenService:GetValue((total_time / Config.Visuals.OnHit.Chams.Duration), Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.In)
                for _, v in pairs(Clone:GetDescendants()) do
                    if v:IsA("MeshPart") or v:IsA("Part") then
                        v.Transparency = fadeValue
                    end
                end
            end)
            task.delay(Config.Visuals.OnHit.Chams.Duration, function()
                if tween then
                    tween:Disconnect()
                end
                Clone:Destroy()
            end)
        end

function Nevermiss:CreateButton(Name, Function)
    do
        local ScreenGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
        local Frame = Instance.new("Frame")
        local TextButton = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
        local TextLabel = Instance.new("TextButton")
        local UITextSizeConstraint = Instance.new("UITextSizeConstraint")

        ScreenGui.Parent = game:GetService("CoreGui")
        ScreenGui.ZIndexBehavior = Enum.ZIndexBehavior.Sibling

        Frame.Parent = ScreenGui
        Frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
        Frame.BackgroundTransparency = 0.3
        Frame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, math.random(-128, 128), 0, 0)
        Frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 90, 0, 32)
        Frame.Active = true

        TextButton.Parent = Frame
        TextButton.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        TextButton.Size = UDim2.new(0, 26, 0, 26)
        TextButton.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0, 0.5)
        TextButton.Position = UDim2.new(0.05, 0, 0.5, 0)
        TextButton.Image = "rbxassetid://10734923214"

        TextLabel.Parent = Frame
        TextLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        TextLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 52, 0, 26)
        TextLabel.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
        TextLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0.65, 0, 0.5, 0)
        TextLabel.Font = Enum.Font.Arimo
        TextLabel.Text = Name
        TextLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        TextLabel.TextScaled = true

        local uiCorner = Instance.new("UICorner", Frame)
        uiCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

        local buttonState = false
        Nevermiss:Connection(TextLabel.MouseButton1Down, function()
            buttonState = not buttonState
            Function(buttonState)
            TextButton.Image = buttonState and "rbxassetid://10735024209" or "rbxassetid://10734923214"
        end)

        local dragging = false
        local dragInput, dragStart, startPos

        local function update(input)
            if not dragStart then return end
            local delta = input.Position - dragStart
            Frame.Position = UDim2.new(startPos.X.Scale, startPos.X.Offset + delta.X, startPos.Y.Scale, startPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y)
        end

        Nevermiss:Connection(Frame.InputBegan, function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                dragging = true
                dragStart = input.Position
                startPos = Frame.Position

                Nevermiss:Connection(input.Changed, function()
                    if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
                        dragging = false
                    end
                end)
            end
        end)

        Nevermiss:Connection(Frame.InputChanged, function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                dragInput = input
            end
        end)

        Nevermiss:Connection(game:GetService("UserInputService").InputChanged, function(input)
            if dragging and input == dragInput then
                update(input)
            end
        end)
    end
end


        function Nevermiss:AutoPrediction()
            if ( Config.Combat.AutoSetup ) then
            pingvalue = Services.Stats.Network.ServerStatsItem['Data Ping']:GetValueString()
            split = string.split(pingvalue,'(')
            ping = tonumber(split[1])

            local X = 0.105 * math.log(ping + 1) +  -0.3295663
            local Y = 0.1 * math.log(ping + 1) +  -0.3255505
            local Z = 0.105 * math.log(ping + 1) +  -0.3295663

            Config.Combat.Prediction.Value[1] = X
            Config.Combat.Prediction.Value[2] = Y
            Config.Combat.Prediction.Value[3] = Z
            end
        end

        function Nevermiss:Spectate()
        if not Config['Anti Aim'].FixCameraSetback then
            if ( Config.Combat.Spectate and Config.Combat.Enabled and Target and Target['Character']['Humanoid']) then
                Camera.CameraSubject = Target['Character']['Humanoid']
            else
                Camera.CameraSubject = LocalPlayer['Character']['Humanoid']
            end
        else
            if ( Config.Combat.Spectate and Config.Combat.Enabled and Target and Target['Character']['Humanoid']) then
                Camera.CameraSubject = Target['Character']['Humanoid']
            else
                Camera.CameraSubject = CameraPart
            end
        end
        end


        function Nevermiss:HitDetection()
            if ( WOAHHH and NEINIGGANEINEI ) then
                local NIGGAAA = WOAHHH
                if ( Config.Visuals.OnHit.Enabled and Target ) then
                    local DamagePosShit = Config.Combat.Hook.Namecall and NIGGAAA[NEINIGGANEINEI] or Target.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Position
                    local GRAHGRAHGRAHKEEPITASTACK = Nevermiss:GetClosestPlayerDamage(DamagePosShit, 20)
                    if ( GRAHGRAHGRAHKEEPITASTACK ) then
                        if ( Config.Visuals.OnHit.Sound.Enabled ) then
                            local Sound = string.format('hitsounds_stuff/%s', Config.Visuals.OnHit.Sound.Value)
                            Nevermiss:PlaySound(getcustomasset(Sound), Config.Visuals.OnHit.Sound.Volume)
                        end
                        
                        if ( Config.Visuals.OnHit.Effect.Enabled ) then
                            Nevermiss:Effect(GRAHGRAHGRAHKEEPITASTACK['Character']['HumanoidRootPart'])
                        end
                        if ( Config.Visuals.OnHit.Chams.Enabled ) then
                            Nevermiss:Hitcham(GRAHGRAHGRAHKEEPITASTACK, Config.Visuals.OnHit.Chams.Color)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end


        function Nevermiss:UpdateAtmosphere()
            if Config.Visuals.World.Enabled and Config.Visuals.World.Rain.Enabled then
                Rain:Enable()
                Rain:SetIntensityRatio(Config.Visuals.World.Rain.Intensity)
                Rain:SetVolume(Config.Visuals.World.Rain.Volume)
                Rain:SetSpeedRatio(Config.Visuals.World.Rain.Speed)
                    Rain:SetColor(Config.Visuals.World.Rain.Color)
            else
                Rain:Disable()
            end
            Services.Lighting.FogColor = Config.Visuals.World.Enabled and Config.Visuals.World.Fog.Enabled and Config.Visuals.World.Fog.Color or Important.World.FogColor
            Services.Lighting.FogStart = Config.Visuals.World.Enabled and Config.Visuals.World.Fog.Enabled and Config.Visuals.World.Fog.Start or Important.World.FogStart
            Services.Lighting.FogEnd = Config.Visuals.World.Enabled and Config.Visuals.World.Fog.Enabled and Config.Visuals.World.Fog.End or Important.World.FogEnd
            Services.Lighting.Ambient = Config.Visuals.World.Enabled and Config.Visuals.World.Ambient.Enabled and Config.Visuals.World.Ambient.Color or Important.World.Ambient
            Services.Lighting.Brightness = Config.Visuals.World.Enabled and Config.Visuals.World.Brightness.Enabled and Config.Visuals.World.Brightness.Value or Important.World.Brightness
            Services.Lighting.ClockTime = Config.Visuals.World.Enabled and Config.Visuals.World.ClockTime.Enabled and Config.Visuals.World.ClockTime.Value or Important.World.ClockTime
            Services.Lighting.ExposureCompensation = Config.Visuals.World.Enabled and Config.Visuals.World.WorldExposure.Enabled and Config.Visuals.World.WorldExposure.Value or Important.World.ExposureCompensation
        end



        function Nevermiss:CalculateOffset(origin, target)
            local actual_origin = origin * CFrame.new(0, Config.Combat['Bullet TP'].Y_Offset, 0, 1, 0, 0, 0, 0, 1, 0, -1, 0);
            return actual_origin:ToObjectSpace(target):inverse();
        end

        function Nevermiss:BulletTP(character)
        local Equipped, Equippedtool, OldPos;

        function Nevermiss:ToolActivated()
        local EquippedTool = LocalPlayer['Character']:FindFirstChildOfClass('Tool')
            OldPos = EquippedTool.Grip
            if ( Config.Combat['Bullet TP'].Enabled and Target ~= nil and Target['Character'] and Config.Combat['Bullet TP'].Activation == 'Tool' ) then
                    if ( Config.Combat['Bullet TP'].Refresh ) then
                        EquippedTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Backpack
                    end
                    if ( Config.Combat['Bullet TP'].Anchor ) then
                        LocalPlayer['Character'].RightHand.Anchored = false
                    end
                    EquippedTool.Grip = Nevermiss:CalculateOffset(LocalPlayer['Character'].RightHand.CFrame, Target['Character'].HumanoidRootPart.CFrame)
                    if ( Config.Combat['Bullet TP'].Anchor ) then
                        LocalPlayer['Character'].RightHand.Anchored = true
                    end
                    if ( Config.Combat['Bullet TP'].Refresh ) then
                        EquippedTool.Parent = LocalPlayer['Character']
                    end
                    Services.RunService.RenderStepped:Wait()
                    if ( Config.Combat['Bullet TP'].Refresh ) then
                        EquippedTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Backpack
                    end
                    if ( Config.Combat['Bullet TP'].Anchor ) then
                        LocalPlayer['Character'].RightHand.Anchored = false
                    end
                    EquippedTool.Grip = OldPos
                    if ( Config.Combat['Bullet TP'].Refresh ) then
                        EquippedTool.Parent = LocalPlayer['Character']
                    end
                end
        end

   
    function Nevermiss:ChildAdded(tool)
        if ( tool:IsA('Tool') and tool.Name ~= 'Nevermiss' and Config.Combat['Bullet TP'].Enabled ) then
            Equippedtool = tool;
            Equipped = Nevermiss:Connection(tool.Activated, function()
                self:ToolActivated()
            end);
        end
    end
   
    function Nevermiss:ChildRemoved(tool)
        if ( tool:IsA('Tool') ) then
            Equippedtool = nil;
            if ( Equipped ) then
                Equipped:Disconnect();
            end
        end
    end

Nevermiss:Connection(character.ChildAdded, function(tool)
    Nevermiss:ChildAdded(tool)
end)

Nevermiss:Connection(character.ChildRemoved, function(tool)
    Nevermiss:ChildRemoved(tool)
end)
end


pcall(function()
    Nevermiss:BulletTP(LocalPlayer['Character'])
end)


Nevermiss:Connection(LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded, function(character)
    Nevermiss:BulletTP(character)
end)


function Nevermiss:GetClosestCenter()
    local Target, Closest = nil, Config.Combat['Auto Target'].Enabled and Config.Combat['Auto Target'].FOV.Size or math.huge

    for _, v in pairs(Services.Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if ( (v['Character'] and v ~= LocalPlayer and v['Character']:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart')) ) then
            local Position, OnScreen = Camera:WorldToScreenPoint(v['Character']['HumanoidRootPart'].Position)
            local Distance = (Vector2.new(Position.X, Position.Y) - (Camera.ViewportSize * 0.5)).Magnitude

            if ( (Distance < Closest and OnScreen) ) then
                Closest = Distance
                Target = v
            end
        end
    end
    return Target or false
end


function Nevermiss:GetClosestToMouse()
    local Target, Closest = nil, Config.Combat['Auto Target'].Enabled and Config.Combat['Auto Target'].FOV.Size or math.huge

    for _, v in pairs(Services.Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if ( (v['Character'] and v ~= LocalPlayer and v['Character']:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart')) ) then
            local Position, OnScreen = Camera:WorldToScreenPoint(v['Character']['HumanoidRootPart'].Position)
            local Distance = (Vector2.new(Position.X, Position.Y) - Vector2.new(Mouse.X, Mouse.Y)).Magnitude

            if ( (Distance < Closest and OnScreen) ) then
                Closest = Distance
                Target = v
            end
        end
    end
    return Target or false
end


do --// ESP functions

-- // Tables
local Visuals = {
    Bases = {},
    Base = {}
}

local Utility = {}

    Conversions = {}
}
local Priorities = {
    2794160137,
}
-- // Flags
Flags = Config.Visuals.ESP
--
function DestroyRenderObject(Obj)  Obj:Remove() end
function SetRenderProperty(Obj, Mod, Value) Obj[Mod] = Value end

--
do -- // Utility
    function Utility:FindInTable(table, name)
        name = name:lower()
        for key, value in pairs(table) do
            if key:lower():find(name) then
                return value
            end
        end
        return "None"
    end
    function Utility:ClampString(String, Length, Font)
        local Font = (Font or 2)
        local Split = String:split("\n")
        --
        local Clamped = ""
        --
        for Index, Value2 in pairs(Split) do
            if (Index * 13) <= Length then
                Clamped = Clamped .. Value2 .. (Index == #Split and "" or "\n")
            end
        end
        --
        return (Clamped ~= String and (Clamped == "" and "" or Clamped:sub(0, #Clamped - 1) .. " ...") or Clamped)
    end
end
--
do -- Color
    function Color:Lerp(Value, MinColor, MaxColor)
        if Value <= 0 then return MaxColor end
        if Value >= 100 then return MinColor end
        --
        return Color3.new(
            MaxColor.R + (MinColor.R - MaxColor.R) * Value,
            MaxColor.G + (MinColor.G - MaxColor.G) * Value,
            MaxColor.B + (MinColor.B - MaxColor.B) * Value
        )
    end
end
--
do -- Math
    do -- Conversions
        Math.Conversions["Studs"] = {
            Conversion = function(Studs)
                return Studs
            end,
            Measurement = "st",
            Round = function(Number)
                return Round(Number)
            end
        }
        --
        Math.Conversions["Meters"] = {
            Conversion = function(Studs)
                return Studs * 0.28
            end,
            Measurement = "m",
            Round = function(Number)
                return Round(Number * 10) / 10
            end
        }
        --
        Math.Conversions["Centimeters"] = {
            Conversion = function(Studs)
                return Studs * 28
            end,
            Measurement = "cm",
            Round = function(Number)
                return Round(Number)
            end
        }
        --
        Math.Conversions["Kilometers"] = {
            Conversion = function(Studs)
                return Studs * 0.00028
            end,
            Measurement = "km",
            Round = function(Number)
                return Round(Number * 1000) / 1000
            end
        }
        --
        Math.Conversions["Millimeters"] = {
            Conversion = function(Studs)
                return Studs * 280
            end,
            Measurement = "mm",
            Round = function(Number)
                return Round(Number)
            end
        }
        --
        Math.Conversions["Micrometers"] = {
            Conversion = function(Studs)
                return Studs * 280000
            end,
            Measurement = "μm",
            Round = function(Number)
                return Round(Number)
            end
        }
        --
        Math.Conversions["Inches"] = {
            Conversion = function(Studs)
                return Studs * 11.0236224
            end,
            Measurement = [['']],
            Round = function(Number)
                return Round(Number)
            end
        }
        --
        Math.Conversions["Miles"] = {
            Conversion = function(Studs)
                return Studs * 0.000173983936
            end,
            Measurement = "mi",
            Round = function(Number)
                return Round(Number * 10000) / 10000
            end

                return Studs * 0399568
            end,
            Measurement = "nmi",
            Round = function(Number)
                return Round(Number * 10000) / 10000
            end
        }

            end,
            Measurement = "yd",
            Round = function(Number)
                return Round(Number * 10) / 10
            end

                return Studs * 0.9186352
            end,
            Measurement = "ft",
            Round = function(Number)
                return Round(Number)
            end
        }
    end
    --
    function Math:RotatePoint(Point, Radians)
        local Unit = Point.Unit
        --
        local Sine = Sin(Radians)
        local Cosine = Cos(Radians)
        --
        return Vector2.new((Cosine * Unit.X) - (Sine * Unit.Y), (Sine * Unit.X) + (Cosine * Unit.Y)).Unit * Point.Magnitude
    end
    --
    function Math:RoundVector(Vector)
        return Vector2.new(Round(Vector.X), Round(Vector.Y))
    end
    --
    function Math:Shift(Number)
        return Acos(Cos(Number * Pi)) / Pi
    end
    --
    function Math:Conversion(Studs, Conversion)
        local Conversion = Math.Conversions[Conversion]
        --
        local Converted = Conversion.Conversion(Studs)
        local Measurement = Conversion.Measurement
        local Rounded = Conversion.Round(Converted)
        --
        return Converted, Measurement, Rounded
    end
    --
    function Math:Random(Number)
        return Random(-Number, Number)
    end
    --
    function Math:RandomVec3(X, Y, Z)
        return Vector3.new(Math:Random(X), Math:Random(Y), Math:Random(Z))
    end
end      
--
do --// Functions
    function Nevermiss:PlayerValid(Player, Function)
        if Player:IsA("Player") then
            if Function then return Function(Player) else return true end
        end
    end
    --
    function Nevermiss:GetCharacter(Player)
        return Player.Character
    end
    --
    function Nevermiss:GetHumanoid(Player, Character)
        return Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
    end
    --
    function Nevermiss:GetHealth(Player, Character, Humanoid)
        if Humanoid then
            return Clamp(Humanoid.Health, 0, Humanoid.MaxHealth), Humanoid.MaxHealth
        end
    end
    --
    function Nevermiss:GetRootPart(Player, Character, Humanoid)
        return Humanoid.RootPart
    end
    --
    function Nevermiss:GetIgnore(Unpacked)
        return
    end
    --
    function Nevermiss:GetBodyParts(Character, RootPart, Indexes, Hitboxes)
        local Parts = {}
        local Hitboxes = Hitboxes or {"Head", "Torso", "Arms", "Legs"}
        --
        for Index, Part in pairs(Character:GetChildren()) do
            if Part:IsA("BasePart") and Part ~= RootPart then
                if Find(Hitboxes, "Head") and Part.Name:lower():find("head") then
                    Parts[Indexes and Part.Name or #Parts + 1] = Part
                elseif Find(Hitboxes, "Torso") and Part.Name:lower():find("torso") then
                    Parts[Indexes and Part.Name or #Parts + 1] = Part
                elseif Find(Hitboxes, "Arms") and Part.Name:lower():find("arm") then
                    Parts[Indexes and Part.Name or #Parts + 1] = Part
                elseif Find(Hitboxes, "Legs") and Part.Name:lower():find("leg") then
                    Parts[Indexes and Part.Name or #Parts + 1] = Part
                elseif (Find(Hitboxes, "Arms") and Part.Name:lower():find("hand")) or (Find(Hitboxes, "Legs ") and Part.Name:lower():find("foot")) then
                    Parts[Indexes and Part.Name or #Parts + 1] = Part
                end
            end
        end
        --
        return Parts
    end
    --
    function Nevermiss:ClientAlive(Player, Character, Humanoid)
        local Health, MaxHealth = Nevermiss:GetHealth(Player, Character, Humanoid)
        --
        return (Health > 0)
    end
    --
    function Nevermiss:ValidateClient(Player)
        local Object = Nevermiss:GetCharacter(Player)
        local Humanoid = (Object and Nevermiss:GetHumanoid(Player, Object))
        local RootPart = (Humanoid and Nevermiss:GetRootPart(Player, Object, Humanoid))
        --
        return Object, Humanoid, RootPart
    end
    --
    function Nevermiss:GetBoundingBox(BodyParts, RootPart)
        local Size = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
        --
        for Index, Value in pairs({"Head", "Torso", "Left Arm", "Right Arm", "Left Leg", "Right Leg"}) do
            local Part = BodyParts[Value]
            local PartSize = (Part and Part.Size or Nevermiss.Locals.PartSizes[Value])
            --
            if Value == "Head" then
                Size = (Size + Vector3.new(0, PartSize.Y, 0))
            elseif Value == "Torso" then
                Size = (Size + Vector3.new(PartSize.X, PartSize.Y, PartSize.Z))
            elseif Value == "Left Arm" then
                Size = (Size + Vector3.new(PartSize.X, 0, 0))
            elseif Value == "Right Arm" then
                Size = (Size + Vector3.new(PartSize.X, 0, 0))
            elseif Value == "Left Leg" then
                Size = (Size + Vector3.new(0, PartSize.Y, 0))
            elseif Value == "Right Leg" then
                Size = (Size + Vector3.new(0, PartSize.Y, 0))
            end
        end
        --
        return (RootPart.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, -0.125, 0)), Size
    end
    --
    function Nevermiss:RayCast(Part, Origin, Ignore, Distance)
        local Ignore = Ignore or {}
        local Distance = Distance or 2000
        --
        local Cast = Ray.new(Origin, (Part.Position - Origin).Unit * Distance)
        local Hit = Workspace:FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(Cast, Ignore)
        --
        return (Hit and Hit:IsDescendantOf(Part.Parent)) == true, Hit
    end
    --
    function Nevermiss:GetPlayers()
        return Services.Players:GetPlayers()
    end
    --
    function Nevermiss:PlayerAdded(Player)
        Visuals:Create({Player = Player})
    end
    --
    function Nevermiss:GetUserID(Player)
        return Player.UserId
    end
    --
    function Nevermiss:GetPlayerParent(Player)
        return Player.Parent
    end
end
--
do -- // Visuals
    function Visuals:Create(Properties)
        if Properties then
            if Properties.Player then
                local Self = DebugTools.SetMetatable({
                    Player = Properties.Player,
                    Highlight = Instance.new("Highlight"),
                    Info = {
                        Tick = os.clock()
                    },
                    Renders = {
                        Flags = Painting.new("Text"),
                        Weapon = Painting.new("Text"),
                        Distance = Painting.new("Text"),
                        HealthBarOutline = Painting.new("Square"),
                        HealthBarInline = Painting.new("Square"),
                        HealthBarValue = Painting.new("Text"),
                        BoxFill = Painting.new("Square"),
                        BoxOutline = Painting.new("Square"),
                        BoxInline = Painting.new("Square"),
                        Name = Painting.new("Text"),
                        Arrow = Painting.new("Triangle"),
                        ArrowOutline = Painting.new("Triangle")
                        
                    }
                }, {
                    __index = Visuals.Base
                })
                --
                Self.Highlight.Parent = Storage
                --
                do -- Renders.Name
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Name, "Text", Self.Player.Name)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Name, "Size", 13)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Name, "Center", true)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Name, "Outline", true)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Name, "Font", 2)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Name, "Visible", false)
                end
                --
                do -- Renders.Box
                    -- Inline
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.BoxInline, "Thickness", 1.25)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.BoxInline, "Filled", false)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.BoxInline, "Visible", false)
                    -- Outline
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.BoxOutline, "Thickness", 2.5)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.BoxOutline, "Filled", false)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.BoxOutline, "Visible", false)
                    -- Fill
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.BoxFill, "Filled", true)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.BoxFill, "Visible", false)
                end
                --
                do -- Renders.HealthBar
                    -- Inline
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.HealthBarInline, "Filled", true)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.HealthBarInline, "Visible", false)
                    -- Outline
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.HealthBarOutline, "Filled", true)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.HealthBarOutline, "Visible", false)
                    -- Value
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.HealthBarValue, "Size", 13)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.HealthBarValue, "Center", false)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.HealthBarValue, "Outline", true)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.HealthBarValue, "Font", 2)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.HealthBarValue, "Visible", false)
                end
                --
                do -- Renders.Flags
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Flags, "Size", 13)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Flags, "Center", false)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Flags, "Outline", true)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Flags, "Font", 2)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Flags, "Visible", false)
                end
                --
                do -- Renders.Distance
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Distance, "Size", 13)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Distance, "Center", true)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Distance, "Outline", true)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Distance, "Font", 2)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Distance, "Visible", false)
                end
                --
                do -- Renders.Weapon
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Weapon, "Size", 13)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Weapon, "Center", true)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Weapon, "Outline", true)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Weapon, "Font", 2)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Weapon, "Visible", false)
                end
                --
                do -- Renders.Arrow
                    -- Inline
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Arrow, "Filled", true)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.Arrow, "Visible", false)
                    -- Outline
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.ArrowOutline, "Filled", false)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.ArrowOutline, "Visible", false)
                    SetRenderProperty(Self.Renders.ArrowOutline, "Thickness", 1.5)
                end
                --
                Visuals.Bases[Properties.Player] = Self
                --
                return Self
            end
        end
    end
    --
    function Visuals:Unload()
        for Index, Value in pairs(Visuals.Bases) do
            Value:Remove()
        end
    end
    --
    function Visuals.Base:Remove()
        local Self = self
        --
        if Self then
            DebugTools.SetMetatable(Self, {})
            --
            Visuals.Bases[Self.Player] = nil
            --
            Self.Object = nil
            --
            for Index, Value in pairs(Self.Renders) do
                DestroyRenderObject(Value)
            end
            --
            Self.Highlight:Remove()
            --
            Self.Renders = nil
            Self.Highlight = nil
            Self = nil
        end
    end
    --
    function Visuals.Base:Opacity(State, Table)
        local Self = self
        --
        if Self then
            local Renders = rawget(Self, "Renders")
            --
            for Index, Value in pairs(typeof(Table) == "table" and Table or Renders) do
                SetRenderProperty(typeof(Table) == "table" and Renders[Value] or Value, "Visible", State)
            end
            --
            Self.Highlight.Adornee = nil
            Self.Highlight.Enabled = false
            --
            if not State then
                Self.Info.RootPartCFrame = nil
                Self.Info.Health = nil
                Self.Info.MaxHealth = nil
                Self.Info.BoundingBox = nil
            end
        end
    end
    --
    function Visuals.Base:Update()
        local Self = self
        --
        if Self then
            local Renders = rawget(Self, "Renders")
            local Player = not Config.Visuals.ESP.Extra.PriorityOnly and rawget(Self, "Player") or Target
            local Player = rawget(Self, "Player")
            local Info = rawget(Self, "Info")

            if Config.Visuals.ESP.Extra.PriorityOnly then
                if Player ~= Target then
                    if Renders then
                        for _, renderObject in pairs(Renders) do
                            if renderObject then
                                SetRenderProperty(renderObject, "Visible", false)
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    Info.Pass = false  -- Prevent rendering for non-targets
                    return
                else
                    Info.Pass = true  -- Ensure target ESP is rendered
                 end
             end
             local Parent = Nevermiss:GetPlayerParent(Player)
            --
            if ( Player and Player ~= LocalPlayer and Parent and Parent ~= nil ) or ( Info.RootPartCFrame and Info.Health and Info.MaxHealth ) then
                if Config.Visuals.ESP.Main.Enabled then
                    local Object, Humanoid, RootPart = Nevermiss:ValidateClient(Player)
                    local BodyParts = (RootPart and Nevermiss:GetBodyParts(Object, RootPart, true))
                    local TransparencyMultplier = 1
                    --
                    if Object and Object.Parent and (Humanoid and RootPart and BodyParts) then
                        local Health, MaxHealth = Nevermiss:GetHealth(Player, Object, Humanoid)
                        --
                        if (Config.Visuals.ESP.Checks.AliveCheck and not Nevermiss:ClientAlive(Player, Character, Humanoid)) or (Config.Visuals.ESP.Checks.ForceField and Object:FindFirstChildOfClass("ForceField")) then 
                            Info.Pass = false
                        else
                            Info.Pass = true
                            Info.RootPartCFrame = RootPart.CFrame
                            Info.Health = Health
                            Info.MaxHealth = MaxHealth
                        end
                    else
                        Info.Pass = false
                    end
                    --
                    if Info.Pass then
                        Info.Tick = os.clock()
                    else
                        local FadeOut = Config.Visuals.ESP.Extra.EspFadeOut
                        local FadeTime = FadeOut / 1000
                        local Value = Info.Tick - os.clock()
                        --
                        if not FadeOut == 0 and Value <= FadeTime then
                            TransparencyMultplier = Clamp((Value + FadeTime) * 1 / FadeTime, 0, 1)
                        else
                            Info.RootPartCFrame = nil
                            Info.Health = nil
                            Info.MaxHealth = nil
                            Info.BoundingBox = nil
                        end
                    end
                    --
                    if Info.RootPartCFrame and Info.Health and Info.MaxHealth then
                        local Override = nil
                        local Orhue, Orsaturation, Orvalue = (Override or Color3.new()):ToHSV()
                        --
                        local Conversion = "Studs"
                        --
                        local Magnitude = (Camera.CFrame.Position - Info.RootPartCFrame.Position).Magnitude
                        local Distance, Measurement, Rounded = Math:Conversion(Magnitude, Conversion)
                        local Position, OnScreen = Services.Workspace.Camera:WorldToViewportPoint(Info.RootPartCFrame.Position)
                        --
                        local BoxSize
                        local BoxPosition 
                        --
                        if OnScreen then
                            local MaxDistance = 2501
                            --
                            if Magnitude <= MaxDistance then
                                local BoundingBox = (Info.Pass and {Nevermiss:GetBoundingBox(BodyParts, RootPart)} or Info.BoundingBox)
                                local Width = (Camera.CFrame - Camera.CFrame.Position) * Vector3.new((Clamp(BoundingBox[2].X, 1, 10) + 0.5) / 2, 0, 0)
                                local Height = (Camera.CFrame - Camera.CFrame.Position) * Vector3.new(0, (Clamp(BoundingBox[2].Y, 1, 10) + 0.5) / 2, 0)
                                --
                                if Info.Pass then
                                    Info.BoundingBox = BoundingBox
                                end
                                --
                                local Middle = Services.Workspace.Camera:WorldToViewportPoint(BoundingBox[1].Position)
                                Width = Abs(Services.Workspace.Camera:WorldToViewportPoint(BoundingBox[1].Position + Width).X - Services.Workspace.Camera:WorldToViewportPoint(BoundingBox[1].Position - Width).X)
                                Height = Abs(Services.Workspace.Camera:WorldToViewportPoint(BoundingBox[1].Position + Height).Y - Services.Workspace.Camera:WorldToViewportPoint(BoundingBox[1].Position - Height).Y)
                                --
                                BoxSize = Math:RoundVector(Vector2.new(Width, Height))
                                BoxPosition = Math:RoundVector(Vector2.new(Middle.X, Middle.Y) - (BoxSize / 2))
                                --
                                do -- Box
                                    if Config.Visuals.ESP.Main.Box.Enabled then
                                        local BoxColor1, BoxTransparency1 = Override or Config.Visuals.ESP.Main.Box.BoxColor, (1 - 0 * TransparencyMultplier)
                                        local BoxColor2, BoxTransparency2 = Override or Config.Visuals.ESP.Main.Box.BoxFillColor, (1 - 0.5 * TransparencyMultplier)
                                        -- Inline
                                        SetRenderProperty(Renders.BoxInline, "Size", BoxSize)
                                        SetRenderProperty(Renders.BoxInline, "Position", BoxPosition)
                                        SetRenderProperty(Renders.BoxInline, "Visible", true)
                                        SetRenderProperty(Renders.BoxInline, "Color", BoxColor1)
                                        SetRenderProperty(Renders.BoxInline, "Transparency", BoxTransparency1)
                                        -- Outline
                                        SetRenderProperty(Renders.BoxOutline, "Size", BoxSize)
                                        SetRenderProperty(Renders.BoxOutline, "Position", BoxPosition)
                                        SetRenderProperty(Renders.BoxOutline, "Visible", true)
                                        SetRenderProperty(Renders.BoxOutline, "Transparency", BoxTransparency1)
                                        -- Fill
                                        SetRenderProperty(Renders.BoxFill, "Size", BoxSize)
                                        SetRenderProperty(Renders.BoxFill, "Position", BoxPosition)
                                        SetRenderProperty(Renders.BoxFill, "Visible", true)
                                        SetRenderProperty(Renders.BoxFill, "Color", BoxColor2)
                                        SetRenderProperty(Renders.BoxFill, "Transparency", BoxTransparency2)
                                    else
                                        SetRenderProperty(Renders.BoxInline, "Visible", false)
                                        SetRenderProperty(Renders.BoxOutline, "Visible", false)
                                        SetRenderProperty(Renders.BoxFill, "Visible", false)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        --
                        do -- Chams
                            if Config.Visuals.ESP.Main.Chams then
                                local ChamsFill, ChamsFillTransparency = Override or Flags[Selection .. "ChamsFill"]:Get().Color, (1 - ((1 - Flags[Selection .. "ChamsFill"]:Get().Transparency) * TransparencyMultplier))
                                local ChamsOutline, ChamsOutlineTransparency = Flags[Selection .. "ChamsOutline"]:Get().Color, (1 - ((1 - Flags[Selection .. "ChamsOutline"]:Get().Transparency) * TransparencyMultplier))
                                local HighlightMode = Flags[Selection .. "HighlightMode"]:Get()
                                --
                                local ChamsAuto = Nevermiss.Locals.SelectedPlayersSection ~= "Local" and Flags[Selection .. "ChamsAuto"]:Get()
                                local ChamsVisible, ChamsVisibleTransparency = ChamsAuto and Flags[Selection .. "ChamsVisible"]:Get().Color, ChamsAuto and (1 - ((1 - Flags[Selection .. "ChamsVisible"]:Get().Transparency) * TransparencyMultplier))
                                local ChamsHidden, ChamsHiddenTransparency = ChamsAuto and Flags[Selection .. "ChamsHidden"]:Get().Color, ChamsAuto and (1 - ((1 - Flags[Selection .. "ChamsHidden"]:Get().Transparency) * TransparencyMultplier))
                                --
                                local Visible = OnScreen and (RootPart ~= nil and Nevermiss:RayCast(RootPart, Camera.CFrame.Position, {Nevermiss:GetCharacter(LocalPlayer), Nevermiss:GetIgnore(true)}))
                                --
                                if Info.Pass then
                                    Self.Highlight.Adornee = Object
                                end
                                --
                                Self.Highlight.FillColor = ChamsAuto and (Visible and ChamsVisible or ChamsHidden) or ChamsFill
                                Self.Highlight.FillTransparency = ChamsAuto and (Visible and ChamsVisibleTransparency or ChamsHiddenTransparency) or ChamsFillTransparency
                                Self.Highlight.OutlineColor = ChamsOutline
                                Self.Highlight.OutlineTransparency = ChamsOutlineTransparency
                                Self.Highlight.DepthMode = Enum.HighlightDepthMode[HighlightMode]
                                Self.Highlight.Enabled = true
                            else
                                Self.Highlight.Adornee = nil
                                Self.Highlight.Enabled = false
                            end
                        end
                        --
                        if BoxSize and BoxPosition then
                            do -- Name
                                local NameEnabled = Config.Visuals.ESP.Main.Name.Enabled
                                --
                                if NameEnabled then
                                    local NameColor, NameTransparency = Override or Config.Visuals.ESP.Main.Name.Color, ((1 - 0) * TransparencyMultplier)
                                    --
                                    local Text
                                    --
                                    if Config.Visuals.ESP.Extra.UseDisplayName then
                                        Text = ((Player.DisplayName ~= nil and Player.DisplayName ~= "" and Player.DisplayName ~= " ") and Player.DisplayName or Player.Name)
                                    else
                                        Text = Player.Name
                                    end
                                    --
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.Name, "Text", Text)
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.Name, "Position", BoxPosition + Vector2.new(BoxSize.X / 2, -(13 + 4)))
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.Name, "Visible", true)
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.Name, "Color", NameColor)
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.Name, "Transparency", NameTransparency)
                                else
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.Name, "Visible", false)
                                end
                            end 
                            --
                            do -- HeatlhBar
                                local HealthBarColor1, HealthBarTransparency = Config.Visuals.ESP.Main.HealthBar.HighHealthColor, ((1 - 0) * TransparencyMultplier)
                                local HealthBarColor2 = Config.Visuals.ESP.Main.HealthBar.LowHealthColor
                                local HealthBarEnabled
                                local HealthNumEnabled
                                --
                                HealthBarEnabled = Config.Visuals.ESP.Main.HealthBar.Enabled
                                HealthNumEnabled = Config.Visuals.ESP.Main.HealthBar.Number
                                --
                                local HealthSize = (Floor(BoxSize.Y * (Info.Health / Info.MaxHealth)))
                                local Color = Color:Lerp(Info.Health / Info.MaxHealth, HealthBarColor1, HealthBarColor2)
                                local Height = ((BoxPosition.Y + BoxSize.Y) - HealthSize)
                                --
                                if HealthBarEnabled then
                                    -- Inline
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.HealthBarInline, "Color", Color)
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.HealthBarInline, "Size", Vector2.new(2, HealthSize))
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.HealthBarInline, "Position", Vector2.new(BoxPosition.X - 5, Height))
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.HealthBarInline, "Visible", true)
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.HealthBarInline, "Transparency", HealthBarTransparency)
                                    -- Outline
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.HealthBarOutline, "Size", Vector2.new(4, BoxSize.Y + 2))
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.HealthBarOutline, "Position", Vector2.new(BoxPosition.X - 6, BoxPosition.Y - 1))
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.HealthBarOutline, "Visible", true)
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.HealthBarOutline, "Transparency", HealthBarTransparency)
                                else
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.HealthBarInline, "Visible", false)
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.HealthBarOutline, "Visible", false)
                                end
                                --
                                if HealthNumEnabled then
                                    -- Value
                                    local Text = Utility:ClampString(tostring(Round(Info.Health)), BoxSize.Y)
                                    --
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.HealthBarValue, "Text", Text)
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.HealthBarValue, "Color", Color)
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.HealthBarValue, "Position", Vector2.new(BoxPosition.X - (HealthBarEnabled and 8 or 4) - (#Text * 8), Clamp(Height, 0, Height + HealthSize - (HealthSize > 13 and 13 or 0))))
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.HealthBarValue, "Visible", true)
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.HealthBarValue, "Transparency", HealthBarTransparency)
                                else
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.HealthBarValue, "Visible", false)
                                end
                            end
                            --
                            local DistanceEnabled = Config.Visuals.ESP.Main.Distance.Enabled
                            local DistanceColor2 = Config.Visuals.ESP.Main.Distance.Color
                            --
                            do -- Distance
                                if DistanceEnabled then
                                    local DistanceColor, DistanceTransparency = Override or DistanceColor2, ((1 - 0) * TransparencyMultplier)
                                    --
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.Distance, "Text", ("%s%s"):format(Rounded, Measurement))
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.Distance, "Position", BoxPosition + Vector2.new(BoxSize.X / 2, (BoxSize.Y + 4)))
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.Distance, "Visible", true)
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.Distance, "Color", DistanceColor)
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.Distance, "Transparency", DistanceTransparency)
                                else
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.Distance, "Visible", false)
                                end
                            end
                            --
                            do -- Weapon
                                local WeaponEnabled = Config.Visuals.ESP.Main.Tool.Enabled
                                local ToolColor = Config.Visuals.ESP.Main.Tool.Color
                                --
                                if WeaponEnabled then
                                    local WeaponColor, WeaponTransparency = Override and Color3.fromHSV(Orhue, Orsaturation, Orvalue - 0.2) or ToolColor, ((1 - 0) * TransparencyMultplier)
                                    --
                                    local Tool = Object:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
                                    --
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.Weapon, "Text", ("%s"):format((Tool and (Tool.Name:sub(0, 12)) or " ")))
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.Weapon, "Position", BoxPosition + Vector2.new(BoxSize.X / 2, (BoxSize.Y + 4 + (DistanceEnabled and 13 or 0))))
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.Weapon, "Visible", true)
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.Weapon, "Color", WeaponColor)
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.Weapon, "Transparency", WeaponTransparency)
                                else
                                    SetRenderProperty(Renders.Weapon, "Visible", false)
                                end
                            end
                            --
                            return
                        end
                    end
                end
                --
                return Self:Opacity(false)
            
            end
            --
            return Self:Remove()
        end
    end
end
--
do -- // Connections
    Nevermiss:Connection(Services.RunService.RenderStepped, LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
        for Index, Value in pairs(Visuals.Bases) do
            Nevermiss:ThreadFunction(function()
                Value:Update()
            end, "3x02")
        end
    end))
    --
    Nevermiss:Connection(Services.Players.ChildAdded, LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(Child)
        Nevermiss:PlayerValid(Child, function(Validated) 
            Nevermiss:PlayerAdded(Validated) 
        end)
    end))
end 
--
for Index, Player in pairs(Nevermiss:GetPlayers()) do
     Nevermiss:PlayerValid(Player, function(Validated) 
        Nevermiss:PlayerAdded(Validated) 
    end)
end

end



function Nevermiss:AutoSelect()
    if Config.Combat['Auto Target'].Enabled then
    Target = Nevermiss:GetClosestCenter()
    end
end


local fire_toggle = false
local automatic_fire = true
local delayshoot = 0.05
Nevermiss:Connection(Services.RunService.Heartbeat, LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
if fire_toggle then
    for _, item in pairs(LocalPlayer.Backpack:GetChildren()) do
        if item:FindFirstChild("GunData") then
            local gunDataModule = item:FindFirstChild("GunData")
            if gunDataModule and gunDataModule:IsA("ModuleScript") then
                local gunData = require(gunDataModule)
                if gunData.cooldown and gunData.slowdown_time then
                    gunData.cooldown = delayshoot
                    gunData.is_automatic = automatic_fire
                    gunData.slowdown_time = delayshoot
                end
            end
        end
    end
    Wait(0)
end
end))

function Nevermiss:HoodCustoms()
    if Config.Combat.Enabled then
        if Config.Combat.Hook.HC then
            local LocalFramework = LocalPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild("Framework", 1e9)

            if LocalFramework then
                local FrameworkEnvironment = getsenv(LocalFramework)

                if FrameworkEnvironment._G and FrameworkEnvironment._G.MOUSE_POSITION then
                    if Target then
                        FrameworkEnvironment._G.MOUSE_POSITION = Nevermiss:TargetPosition().Position
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
end

Nevermiss:Connection(Services.RunService.PreSimulation, LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    Nevermiss:ThreadFunction(function()
        Nevermiss:HitDetection()
        Nevermiss:UpdateHealth()
        Nevermiss:ShootSound()
        Nevermiss:AutoPrediction()
        Nevermiss:UpdateAtmosphere()
        Nevermiss:Spectate()
        Nevermiss:UpdateFieldOfView()
        Nevermiss:AutoSelect()
    end, 'PreSimulation Thread')
end))
Nevermiss:Connection(Services.RunService.PostSimulation, LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
    Nevermiss:ThreadFunction(function()
        Nevermiss:UpdateTargetVisuals()
        Nevermiss:HoodCustoms()
        Nevermiss:LookAt()
        Nevermiss:CSync()
        Nevermiss:Resolve()
    end, 'PostSimulation Thread')
end))

local Prediction_Convertion = {
    Enabled = false,
    Value = '0.135',
    Clipboard = true,
    Notify = true,
    NotifyLength = '10',
}


function Nevermiss:ConvertPrediction()
    if Prediction_Convertion.Enabled then
        local Prediction_Value = Prediction_Convertion.Value
        local Formula = tonumber(1/Prediction_Value)
        if Prediction_Convertion.Notify then
            Library:Notify([[N<font color="rgb(18, 85, 92)">e</font>ver<font color="rgb(18, 85, 92)">miss</font> | ]] .. Prediction_Convertion.Value .. ' to ' .. Formula, Prediction_Convertion.NotifyLength)
        end
        if Prediction_Convertion.Clipboard then
            setclipboard(Formula)
        end
    end
end

for i, v in getgc(true) do
    if type(v) == "table" and rawget(v, "getAim") then
        local OldGetAim = v.getAim
        v.getAim = function(Vector)
            if Target and Config.Combat.Hook.Override_Aim then
                local HitPos = Nevermiss:TargetPosition().Position
                return (HitPos - Vector).unit
            end
            return OldGetAim(Vector)
        end
    end
end

local NamecallHook
NamecallHook = hookmetamethod(game, '__namecall', LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(Self, ...)
    local Arguments = {...}
    local Method = tostring(getnamecallmethod())
    if ( Config.Combat.Hook.Namecall and not Config.Combat.Hook.HC ) then
        if ( not checkcaller() and Method == 'FireServer' ) then
            for i, Argument in pairs(Arguments) do
                if ( typeof(Argument) == 'Vector3' ) then
                    WOAHHH = Arguments
                    NEINIGGANEINEI = i
                    if ( Config.Combat.Enabled and Target ~= nil ) then
                        Arguments[i] = Nevermiss:TargetPosition().Position
                    end
                end
            end
            return NamecallHook(Self, unpack(Arguments))
        end
    end
    return NamecallHook(Self, ...)
end))

local mt = getrawmetatable(game)
local backupindex = mt.__index
setreadonly(mt, false)
mt.__index = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(t, k)
    if ( (t:IsA("Mouse") and (k == "Hit" or k == "Target")) and Config.Combat.Enabled and Target ~= nil and Config.Combat.Hook.Metatable_Mouse and not Config.Combat.Hook.HC ) then
            local position = Nevermiss:TargetPosition()
            return (k == "Hit" and position or position.Position)
    end
    return backupindex(t, k)
end)
setreadonly(mt, true)

local IndexMousePos
IndexMousePos = hookmetamethod(LocalPlayer:GetMouse(), '__index', LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(self, index)
    if ( (index == 'Hit' ) and Config.Combat.Enabled and Target ~= nil and Config.Combat.Hook.Index and not Config.Combat.Hook.HC ) then
            local position = Nevermiss:TargetPosition()
            return ( position )
    end
    return IndexMousePos(self, index)
end))

    Title = [[N<font color="rgb(18, 85, 92)">e</font>ver<font color="rgb(18, 85, 92)">miss</font>]],
    Center = true,
    AutoShow = true,
    TabPadding = 8,
    MenuFadeTime = 0.2,
})
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        local duration = 1.5
        local steps = 60
        local stepTime = duration / steps
        
        for i = 0, 1, 1 / steps do
            local t = (math.sin(i * math.pi - math.pi / 2) + 1) / 2
            
            local r = math.floor(18 + (255 - 18) * t)
            local g = math.floor(85 + (255 - 85) * t)
            local b = math.floor(92 + (255 - 92) * t)
            
            local color = string.format("rgb(%d, %d, %d)", r, g, b)
            local title = string.format([[N<font color="%s">e</font>ver<font color="%s">miss</font>]], color, color)
            
            Window:SetWindowTitle(title)
            Wait(stepTime)
        end

        for i = 1, 0, -1 / steps do
            local t = (math.sin(i * math.pi - math.pi / 2) + 1) / 2
            
            local r = math.floor(18 + (255 - 18) * t)
            local g = math.floor(85 + (255 - 85) * t)
            local b = math.floor(92 + (255 - 92) * t)
            
            local color = string.format("rgb(%d, %d, %d)", r, g, b)
            local title = string.format([[N<font color="%s">e</font>ver<font color="%s">miss</font>]], color, color)
            
            Window:SetWindowTitle(title)
            Wait(stepTime)
        end
    end
end)

local dragging
local dragInput
local dragStart
local startPos
function update(input)
        local delta = input.Position - dragStart
        frame.Position = UDim2.new(startPos.X.Scale, startPos.X.Offset + delta.X, startPos.Y.Scale, startPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y)
end
Nevermiss:Connection(frame.InputBegan, function(input)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            dragging = true
            dragStart = input.Position
            startPos = frame.Position
                               Nevermiss:Connection(input.Changed, function()
                if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
                    dragging = false
                end
            end)
        end
end)
Nevermiss:Connection(frame.InputChanged, function(input)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            dragInput = input
        end
    end)
Nevermiss:Connection(Services.UserInputService.InputChanged, function(input)
        if input == dragInput and dragging then
            update(input)
        end
end)

                Text = 'Button',

                if ( RButton ) then
                    return

do --// Exclusive

            Text = 'Fire Rate',

            Tooltip = 'PP.',

            Callback = function(Value)
                fire_toggle = Value
            end
        })
        local FireRateCFG = Hood_Customs:AddDependencyBox();
        FireRateCFG:AddToggle('Monkey', {
            Text = 'Automatic',
            Default = true,
            Tooltip = 'PP.',

            Callback = function(Value)
                automatic_fire = Value
            end
        })
        FireRateCFG:AddInput('The2ndSheet', {
            Default = '0.05',
            Numeric = true,
            Finished = true,
            Text = 'Cooldown',
            Tooltip = 'Cooldown Shit',
            Placeholder = 'no',

            Callback = function(Value)
                delayshoot = tonumber(Value)
            end
        })
        FireRateCFG:SetupDependencies({
            { Toggles.FireShit, true }
        });
    end

do --// UI Settings
local MenuGroup = Tabs['UI Settings']:AddLeftGroupbox('Menu')

SaveManager:IgnoreThemeSettings()
SaveManager:SetIgnoreIndexes({ 'MenuKeybind' })
SaveManager:SetFolder('Nevermiss')
SaveManager:SetLibrary(Library)
-- Builds our config menu on the right side of our tab
SaveManager:BuildConfigSection(Tabs['UI Settings'])

-- Builds our theme menu (with plenty of built in themes) on the left side
-- NOTE: you can also call ThemeManager:ApplyToGroupbox to add it to a specific groupbox
-- You can use the SaveManager:LoadAutoloadConfig() to load a config
-- which has been marked to be one that auto loads!
SaveManager:LoadAutoloadConfig()

end
end
print("GUI took "..time()-UiLoadSpeed.." seconds to load in.")
end)
